```
class Word:
    """Represents a single word entry."""
    def __init__(self, data: Dict[str, str]):
        self.word = data["word"].strip().lower()
        self.lemma = data["lemma"].strip().lower()
        self.pos = data["pos"].strip().lower()
        self.definition = data["definition"].strip()
        self.en_example = data["en_example"].strip()
        self.tr_translation = data["tr_translation"].strip()
        self.tr_example = data["tr_example"].strip()
        self.frequency_rank = int(data["frequency_rank"])

    def to_dict(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        return {
            "word": self.word,
            "lemma": self.lemma,
            "pos": self.pos,
            "definition": self.definition,
            "en_example": self.en_example,
            "tr_translation": self.tr_translation,
            "tr_example": self.tr_example,
            "frequency_rank": self.frequency_rank,
        }

class SRS:
    """Simple Spaced Repetition System (SRS-lite)."""
    def __init__(self):
        self.stability: Dict[str, float] = {}  # Ease factor (1.0-2.5)
        self.last_seen: Dict[str, str] = {}    # ISO date
        self.due_date: Dict[str, str] = {}     # Next review date

    def update(self, word: str, knew: bool, ease: float = 2.5) -> None:
        """Update SRS metrics based on user response."""
        if knew:
            self.stability[word] = min(2.5, self.stability.get(word, 1.0) + 0.2)
            interval_days = int(self.stability[word] * 3)  # Simple interval
        else:
            self.stability[word] = max(1.0, self.stability.get(word, 1.0) - 0.3)
            interval_days = 1
        today = datetime.now().isoformat()[:10]
        self.last_seen[word] = today
        next_due = (datetime.now() + timedelta(days=interval_days)).isoformat()[:10]
        self.due_date[word] = next_due

    def is_due(self, word: str) -> bool:
        """Check if word is due for review."""
        due = self.due_date.get(word)
        if not due:
            return True  # New words are due
        return datetime.now().isoformat()[:10] >= due

    def get_next_words(self, words: List[Word], daily_goal: int = 20, pos_filter: Optional[str] = None) -> List[Word]:
        """Get next words for session: new + due reviews, filtered by POS/freq."""
        today = datetime.now().isoformat()[:10]
        candidates = []
        for w in sorted(words, key=lambda x: x.frequency_rank):  # Low rank (frequent) first
            if pos_filter and w.pos != pos_filter:
                continue
            if self.is_due(w.word):
                candidates.append(w)
                if len(candidates) >= daily_goal:
                    break
        return candidates

    def to_dict(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        return {
            "stability": self.stability,
            "last_seen": self.last_seen,
            "due_date": self.due_date,
        }

    @classmethod
    def from_dict(cls, data: Dict[str, Any]) -> 'SRS':
        srs = cls()
        srs.stability = data.get("stability", {})
        srs.last_seen = data.get("last_seen", {})
        srs.due_date = data.get("due_date", {})
        return srs

class Progress:
    """User progress tracker."""
    def __init__(self, username: str = "Guest"):
        self.username = username
        self.correct = 0
        self.incorrect = 0
        self.daily_streak = 0
        self.learned_words = set()
        self.mode_stats = {"flashcards": 0, "mc": 0, "write": 0, "speed": 0}
        self.badges = []  # e.g., "100 words learned"
        self.srs = SRS()

    def update_score(self, correct: bool) -> None:
        if correct:
            self.correct += 1
            if self.correct + self.incorrect > 0 and self.correct / (self.correct + self.incorrect) > 0.8:
                self.daily_streak += 1
            if len(self.learned_words) % 100 == 0 and len(self.learned_words) > 0:
                self.badges.append(f"{len(self.learned_words)} kelimeyi öğrendin!")
        else:
            self.incorrect += 1
            self.daily_streak = 0

    def mark_learned(self, word: str) -> None:
        self.learned_words.add(word)
        self.srs.update(word, True)

    def to_dict(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        return {
            "username": self.username,
            "correct": self.correct,
            "incorrect": self.incorrect,
            "daily_streak": self.daily_streak,
            "learned_words": list(self.learned_words),
            "mode_stats": self.mode_stats,
            "badges": self.badges,
            "srs": self.srs.to_dict(),
        }

    @classmethod
    def from_dict(cls, data: Dict[str, Any]) -> 'Progress':
        prog = cls(data.get("username", "Guest"))
        prog.correct = data.get("correct", 0)
        prog.incorrect = data.get("incorrect", 0)
        prog.daily_streak = data.get("daily_streak", 0)
        prog.learned_words = set(data.get("learned_words", []))
        prog.mode_stats = data.get("mode_stats", {"flashcards": 0, "mc": 0, "write": 0, "speed": 0})
        prog.badges = data.get("badges", [])
        prog.srs = SRS.from_dict(data.get("srs", {}))
        return prog

def load_progress(path: str) -> Progress:
    """Load progress from JSON, with error handling."""
    if not os.path.exists(path):
        return Progress()
    try:
        with open(path, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
            data = json.load(f)
        return Progress.from_dict(data)
    except (json.JSONDecodeError, KeyError) as e:
        messagebox.showwarning("Uyarı", f"İlerleme dosyası bozuk: {e}. Yeni profil başlatılıyor.")
        return Progress()

def save_progress(prog: Progress, path: str) -> None:
    """Save progress to JSON."""
    os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(path), exist_ok=True)
    with open(path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        json.dump(prog.to_dict(), f, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)

def load_words(csv_path: str = "data/words_2000.csv") -> List[Word]:
    """Load words from CSV asynchronously."""
    words = EMBEDDED_WORDS.copy()  # Fallback
    if os.path.exists(csv_path):
        try:
            with open(csv_path, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
                reader = csv.DictReader(f)
                if set(reader.fieldnames) != {"word", "lemma", "pos", "definition", "en_example", "tr_translation", "tr_example", "frequency_rank"}:
                    raise ValueError("CSV sütunları eksik veya yanlış.")
                words = [Word(row) for row in reader]
        except Exception as e:
            messagebox.showerror("Hata", f"CSV yüklenemedi: {e}. Gömülü kelimeler kullanılıyor.")
    return [Word(w) for w in words]

class GameMode:
    """Base class for game modes."""
    def __init__(self, root, words: List[Word], progress: Progress):
        self.root = root
        self.words = words
        self.progress = progress
        self.current_index = 0
        self.current_word = None
        self.score = 0
        self.streak = 0

    def start(self) -> None:
        raise NotImplementedError

    def next_word(self) -> None:
        raise NotImplementedError

    def submit(self, user_input: Any) -> bool:
        raise NotImplementedError

class Flashcards(GameMode):
    """Flashcards mode: EN front, TR back."""
    def __init__(self, root, words: List[Word], progress: Progress):
        super().__init__(root, words, progress)
        self.flipped = False
        self.canvas = None  # To be set in UI
        self.knew_btn = None
        self.unknown_btn = None

    def start(self) -> None:
        self.next_word()
        self.root.bind("<space>", lambda e: self.flip())
        self.root.bind("b", lambda e: self.knew())
        self.root.bind("n", lambda e: self.unknown())
        self.root.bind("<Return>", lambda e: self.next_word())

    def next_word(self) -> None:
        self.current_word = self.words[self.current_index % len(self.words)]
        self.flipped = False
        self.update_display()
        self.current_index += 1

    def update_display(self) -> None:
        if not self.canvas:
            return
        if not self.flipped:
            text = f"{self.current_word.word} ({self.current_word.pos})\n{self.current_word.definition}\nÖrnek: {self.current_word.en_example}"
            if self.knew_btn and self.unknown_btn:
                self.knew_btn.pack_forget()
                self.unknown_btn.pack_forget()
        else:
            text = f"Türkçe: {self.current_word.tr_translation}\nÖrnek: {self.current_word.tr_example}"
            if self.knew_btn and self.unknown_btn:
                self.knew_btn.pack(side=tk.LEFT, padx=20)
                self.unknown_btn.pack(side=tk.RIGHT, padx=20)
        self.canvas.delete("all")
        self.canvas.create_text(250, 250, text=text, font=("Arial", 12))

    def flip(self) -> None:
        self.flipped = not self.flipped
        self.update_display()

    def knew(self) -> None:
        self.progress.srs.update(self.current_word.word, True)
        self.progress.mark_learned(self.current_word.word)
        self.progress.update_score(True)
        self.progress.mode_stats["flashcards"] += 1
        self.next_word()

    def unknown(self) -> None:
        self.progress.srs.update(self.current_word.word, False)
        self.progress.update_score(False)
        self.progress.mode_stats["flashcards"] += 1
        self.next_word()

class MultipleChoice(GameMode):
    """Multiple Choice EN→TR (with reverse option)."""
    def __init__(self, root, words: List[Word], progress: Progress, reverse: bool = False):
        super().__init__(root, words, progress)
        self.reverse = reverse
        self.options = []
        self.correct_idx = 0
        self.buttons = []
        self.question_label = None

    def start(self, reverse: bool = False) -> None:
        self.reverse = reverse
        self.root.unbind("<space>")
        self.root.unbind("b")
        self.root.unbind("n")
        for i in range(1, 5):
            self.root.bind(str(i), lambda e, idx=i-1: self.submit(idx))
        self.root.bind("<Return>", lambda e: self.next_word())  # Next after submit
        self.next_word()

    def next_word(self) -> None:
        self.current_word = self.words[self.current_index % len(self.words)]
        distractors = [w for w in self.words if w.pos == self.current_word.pos and w.word != self.current_word.word][:3]
        if len(distractors) < 3:
            distractors = random.sample([w for w in self.words if w.word != self.current_word.word], min(3, len(self.words)-1))
        options = [self.current_word.tr_translation] + [d.tr_translation for d in distractors]
        random.shuffle(options)
        self.options = options
        self.correct_idx = options.index(self.current_word.tr_translation)
        self.current_index += 1
        self.update_display()

    def update_display(self) -> None:
        if not self.question_label:
            return
        question = f"Türkçe nedir? {self.current_word.word}" if not self.reverse else f"İngilizce nedir? {self.current_word.tr_translation}"
        self.question_label.config(text=question)
        for i, btn in enumerate(self.buttons):
            if i < len(self.options):
                btn.config(text=self.options[i])
                btn.pack(pady=5)
            else:
                btn.pack_forget()

    def submit(self, choice: int) -> bool:
        correct = choice == self.correct_idx
        self.progress.update_score(correct)
        if correct:
            self.progress.mark_learned(self.current_word.word)
            self.progress.mode_stats["mc"] += 1
        # Visual feedback: green/red frame (simplified)
        self.root.configure(bg="lightgreen" if correct else "lightcoral")
        self.root.after(500, lambda: self.root.configure(bg="SystemButtonFace"))
        self.streak = self.streak + 1 if correct else 0
        self.root.after(500, self.next_word)
        return correct

class WriteIt(GameMode):
    """Write-It: TR→EN spelling with tolerance."""
    def __init__(self, root, words: List[Word], progress: Progress, tolerance: int = 2):
        super().__init__(root, words, progress)
        self.tolerance = tolerance
        self.entry = None  # To be set in UI
        self.question_label = None

    def start(self) -> None:
        self.next_word()
        self.root.bind("<Return>", lambda e: self.submit())

    def next_word(self) -> None:
        self.current_word = self.words[self.current_index % len(self.words)]
        if self.entry:
            self.entry.delete(0, tk.END)
        self.current_index += 1
        self.update_display()

    def update_display(self) -> None:
        if self.question_label:
            self.question_label.config(text=f"İngilizce yaz: {self.current_word.tr_translation}")

    def submit(self) -> bool:
        user = self.entry.get().strip().lower() if self.entry else ""
        # Normalize: remove accents, etc.
        user_norm = ''.join(c for c in unicodedata.normalize('NFD', user) if unicodedata.category(c) != 'Mn')
        target_norm = ''.join(c for c in unicodedata.normalize('NFD', self.current_word.word) if unicodedata.category(c) != 'Mn')
        # Allow plural/s if applicable (simple check)
        target_patterns = [re.escape(target_norm), re.escape(target_norm) + 's?']
        matched = any(re.match(f'^({pattern})$', user_norm) for pattern in target_patterns)
        if not matched:
            dist = levenshtein_distance(user_norm, target_norm)
            correct = dist <= self.tolerance
            if 1 <= dist <= self.tolerance - 1:
                messagebox.showinfo("Yakın!", "Yakın! Tekrar dene.")
        else:
            correct = True
        self.progress.update_score(correct)
        if correct:
            self.progress.mark_learned(self.current_word.word)
            self.progress.mode_stats["write"] += 1
        # Visual feedback
        self.root.configure(bg="lightgreen" if correct else "lightcoral")
        self.root.after(500, lambda: self.root.configure(bg="SystemButtonFace"))
        self.root.after(500, self.next_word)
        return correct

class SpeedRound(GameMode):
    """Speed Round: Timed quiz."""
    def __init__(self, root, words: List[Word], progress: Progress, duration: int = 30):
        super().__init__(root, words, progress)
        self.duration = duration
        self.time_left = duration
        self.timer_id = None
        self.mc_mode = MultipleChoice(root, words, progress)
        self.timer_label = None

    def start(self) -> None:
        self.mc_mode.start()
        self.time_left = self.duration
        self.update_timer()
        self.tick()

    def tick(self) -> None:
        self.time_left -= 1
        self.update_timer()
        if self.time_left > 0:
            self.timer_id = self.root.after(1000, self.tick)
        else:
            self.end_round()

    def update_timer(self) -> None:
        if self.timer_label:
            self.timer_label.config(text=f"Zaman: {self.time_left}s")

    def submit(self, choice: int) -> bool:
        correct = self.mc_mode.submit(choice)
        if correct:
            self.score += 1 + (self.streak // 5)  # Streak bonus
            self.progress.mode_stats["speed"] += 1
        self.mc_mode.next_word()  # Immediate next
        return correct

    def end_round(self) -> None:
        messagebox.showinfo("Bitti!", f"Skor: {self.score}")
        if self.timer_id:
            self.root.after_cancel(self.timer_id)

class WordGameApp:
    """Main application class."""
    def __init__(self, root):
        self.root = root
        self.root.title("İngilizce-Türkçe Kelime Oyunu")
        self.root.geometry("800x600")
        self.words: List[Word] = []
        self.progress = Progress()
        self.current_mode: Optional[GameMode] = None
        self.daily_goal = 20
        self.tolerance = 2
        self.theme = "light"  # or "dark"
        self.zoom = 1.0
        self.pos_filter = None
        self.reverse_mc = False
        self.load_data()
        self.setup_ui()
        self.apply_theme()
        self.root.protocol("WM_DELETE_WINDOW", self.on_closing)

    def load_data(self) -> None:
        """Load words and progress asynchronously."""
        def _load():
            self.words = load_words()
            self.progress = load_progress("storage/progress.json")
            self.root.after(0, self.on_data_loaded)
        threading.Thread(target=_load, daemon=True).start()

    def on_data_loaded(self) -> None:
        # Update next words based on SRS
        self.words = self.progress.srs.get_next_words(self.words, self.daily_goal, self.pos_filter)
        self.update_stats()

    def setup_ui(self) -> None:
        """Setup main UI: menu, left panel (modes), right panel (stats), center (game)."""
        # Menu
        menubar = tk.Menu(self.root)
        self.root.config(menu=menubar)

        file_menu = tk.Menu(menubar, tearoff=0)
        menubar.add_cascade(label="Dosya", menu=file_menu)
        file_menu.add_command(label="CSV İçe Aktar", command=self.import_csv)
        file_menu.add_command(label="İlerlemeyi Dışa Aktar", command=self.export_progress)
        file_menu.add_separator()
        file_menu.add_command(label="Çıkış", command=self.root.quit)

        settings_menu = tk.Menu(menubar, tearoff=0)
        menubar.add_cascade(label="Ayarlar", menu=settings_menu)
        settings_menu.add_command(label="Günlük Hedef", command=self.set_goal)
        settings_menu.add_command(label="Yazım Toleransı", command=self.set_tolerance)
        settings_menu.add_command(label="Koyu Tema", command=self.toggle_theme)
        settings_menu.add_command(label="Ters Mod (Çoktan Seçmeli)", command=self.toggle_reverse)

        view_menu = tk.Menu(menubar, tearoff=0)
        menubar.add_cascade(label="Görünüm", menu=view_menu)
        view_menu.add_command(label="Büyüt", command=lambda: self.zoom_in())
        view_menu.add_command(label="Küçült", command=lambda: self.zoom_out())
        view_menu.add_command(label="Sıfırla", command=lambda: self.zoom_reset())

        help_menu = tk.Menu(menubar, tearoff=0)
        menubar.add_cascade(label="Yardım", menu=help_menu)
        help_menu.add_command(label="Kısayollar", command=self.show_shortcuts)
        help_menu.add_command(label="Hakkında", command=self.show_about)

        # Left panel: Mode selection
        left_frame = ttk.Frame(self.root)
        left_frame.pack(side=tk.LEFT, fill=tk.Y, padx=10, pady=10)
        modes = ["Kart Ezber", "Çoktan Seçmeli", "Yaz-Boz", "Hız Turu"]
        for mode in modes:
            btn = ttk.Button(left_frame, text=mode, command=lambda m=mode: self.start_mode(m))
            btn.pack(pady=5)

        # Right panel: Stats
        stats_frame = ttk.Frame(self.root)
        stats_frame.pack(side=tk.RIGHT, fill=tk.Y, padx=10, pady=10)
        self.stats_label = ttk.Label(stats_frame, text="İstatistikler\nDoğru: 0\nYanlış: 0\nSeri: 0\nÖğrenilen: 0\nRozetler: Yok", justify=tk.LEFT)
        self.stats_label.pack()
        self.progress_bar = ttk.Progressbar(stats_frame, maximum=self.daily_goal, orient=tk.HORIZONTAL)
        self.progress_bar.pack(fill=tk.X, pady=10)

        # Center: Game area
        self.center_frame = ttk.Frame(self.root)
        self.center_frame.pack(expand=True, fill=tk.BOTH, padx=10, pady=10)
        self.game_label = ttk.Label(self.center_frame, text="Mod Seçin")
        self.game_label.pack(expand=True)

    def start_mode(self, mode_name: str) -> None:
        """Start selected game mode."""
        for widget in self.center_frame.winfo_children():
            widget.destroy()
        if mode_name == "Kart Ezber":
            self.current_mode = Flashcards(self.root, self.words, self.progress)
            self.current_mode.canvas = tk.Canvas(self.center_frame, width=500, height=400, bg="white")
            self.current_mode.canvas.pack(expand=True)
            self.current_mode.knew_btn = ttk.Button(self.center_frame, text="Biliyordum", command=self.current_mode.knew)
            self.current_mode.unknown_btn = ttk.Button(self.center_frame, text="Bilmiyordum", command=self.current_mode.unknown)
            self.current_mode.start()
        elif mode_name == "Çoktan Seçmeli":
            self.current_mode = MultipleChoice(self.root, self.words, self.progress, self.reverse_mc)
            self.current_mode.question_label = ttk.Label(self.center_frame, text="", font=("Arial", 12))
            self.current_mode.question_label.pack(pady=20)
            self.current_mode.buttons = [ttk.Button(self.center_frame, text="", command=lambda i=i: self.current_mode.submit(i)) for i in range(4)]
            self.current_mode.start(self.reverse_mc)
        elif mode_name == "Yaz-Boz":
            self.current_mode = WriteIt(self.root, self.words, self.progress, self.tolerance)
            self.current_mode.question_label = ttk.Label(self.center_frame, text="", font=("Arial", 12))
            self.current_mode.question_label.pack(pady=20)
            self.current_mode.entry = ttk.Entry(self.center_frame, font=("Arial", 12 * self.zoom), width=30)
            self.current_mode.entry.pack(pady=10)
            submit_btn = ttk.Button(self.center_frame, text="Gönder", command=self.current_mode.submit)
            submit_btn.pack()
            self.current_mode.start()
        elif mode_name == "Hız Turu":
            duration = 30 if self.daily_goal > 20 else 60  # Adjust based on goal
            self.current_mode = SpeedRound(self.root, self.words, self.progress, duration)
            self.current_mode.mc_mode.question_label = ttk.Label(self.center_frame, text="", font=("Arial", 12))
            self.current_mode.mc_mode.question_label.pack(pady=20)
            self.current_mode.mc_mode.buttons = [ttk.Button(self.center_frame, text="", command=lambda i=i: self.current_mode.submit(i)) for i in range(4)]
            for btn in self.current_mode.mc_mode.buttons:
                btn.pack(pady=5)
            self.current_mode.timer_label = ttk.Label(self.center_frame, text="")
            self.current_mode.timer_label.pack()
            self.current_mode.start()
        self.update_stats()

    def update_stats(self) -> None:
        learned = len(self.progress.learned_words)
        badges_text = "\n".join(self.progress.badges[-3:]) if self.progress.badges else "Yok"
        self.stats_label.config(text=f"İstatistikler\nDoğru: {self.progress.correct}\nYanlış: {self.progress.incorrect}\nSeri: {self.progress.daily_streak}\nÖğrenilen: {learned}\nRozetler:\n{badges_text}")
        self.progress_bar["value"] = min(learned, self.daily_goal)

    def import_csv(self) -> None:
        path = filedialog.askopenfilename(filetypes=[("CSV", "*.csv")])
        if path:
            def _import():
                new_words = load_words(path)
                self.words = self.progress.srs.get_next_words(new_words, self.daily_goal, self.pos_filter)
                self.root.after(0, lambda: messagebox.showinfo("Başarılı", "CSV yüklendi!"))
                self.root.after(0, self.update_stats)
            threading.Thread(target=_import, daemon=True).start()

    def export_progress(self) -> None:
        path = filedialog.asksaveasfilename(defaultextension=".json", filetypes=[("JSON", "*.json"), ("CSV", "*.csv")])
        if path:
            if path.endswith(".csv"):
                # Export to CSV: word,learned_date, etc. (simple)
                with open(path, "w", newline="", encoding="utf-8") as f:
                    writer = csv.writer(f)
                    writer.writerow(["word", "learned"])
                    for w in self.progress.learned_words:
                        writer.writerow([w, datetime.now().isoformat()[:10]])
            else:
                save_progress(self.progress, path)
            messagebox.showinfo("Başarılı", "İlerleme dışa aktarıldı.")

    def set_goal(self) -> None:
        goal = simpledialog.askinteger("Günlük Hedef", "Hedef kelime sayısı:", initialvalue=self.daily_goal)
        if goal:
            self.daily_goal = goal
            self.progress_bar["maximum"] = self.daily_goal
            self.on_data_loaded()

    def set_tolerance(self) -> None:
        tol = simpledialog.askinteger("Tolerans", "Yazım hatası toleransı (0-5):", initialvalue=self.tolerance)
        if tol:
            self.tolerance = tol

    def toggle_theme(self) -> None:
        self.theme = "dark" if self.theme == "light" else "light"
        self.apply_theme()

    def toggle_reverse(self) -> None:
        self.reverse_mc = not self.reverse_mc
        messagebox.showinfo("Ters Mod", f"Ters mod: {'Açık' if self.reverse_mc else 'Kapalı'} (TR→EN)")

    def apply_theme(self) -> None:
        style = ttk.Style()
        if self.theme == "dark":
            style.theme_use("clam")
            bg = "#2b2b2b"
            fg = "#ffffff"
        else:
            bg = "#ffffff"
            fg = "#000000"
        self.root.configure(bg=bg)
        style.configure("TLabel", background=bg, foreground=fg)
        style.configure("TButton", background=bg, foreground=fg)
        style.configure("TFrame", background=bg)
        style.configure("TEntry", fieldbackground=bg, foreground=fg)
        style.configure("TProgressbar", background=fg)

    def zoom_in(self) -> None:
        self.zoom *= 1.1
        self.apply_zoom()

    def zoom_out(self) -> None:
        self.zoom /= 1.1
        self.apply_zoom()

    def zoom_reset(self) -> None:
        self.zoom = 1.0
        self.apply_zoom()

    def apply_zoom(self) -> None:
        font_size = int(12 * self.zoom)
        default_font = ("Arial", font_size)
        self.root.option_add("*Font", default_font)
        # Update existing labels if possible
        for widget in self.root.winfo_children():
            if isinstance(widget, ttk.Label):
                widget.configure(font=default_font)

    def show_shortcuts(self) -> None:
        messagebox.showinfo("Kısayollar", "Enter: Onay/Flip\nSpace: Flip\n1-4: Seçenekler\nB: Biliyordum\nN: Bilmiyordum")

    def show_about(self) -> None:
        messagebox.showinfo("Hakkında", "İngilizce-Türkçe Kelime Oyunu v1.0\nEğitim amaçlı geliştirildi.")

    def on_closing(self) -> None:
        save_progress(self.progress, "storage/progress.json")
        self.root.destroy()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    root = tk.Tk()
    app = WordGameApp(root)
    root.mainloop()
```

README.md
```
# İngilizce-Türkçe Kelime Oyunu

Bu, Tkinter tabanlı bağımsız bir GUI uygulamasıdır. İngilizce kelimeleri Türkçe karşılıklarıyla öğrenmek için tasarlanmıştır. 4 oyun modu, aralıklı tekrar (SRS) ve ilerleme takibi içerir.

## Kurulum
1. Python 3.10+ yükleyin.
2. `data/words_2000.csv` şablonunu kendi 2000 kelimelik listenizle değiştirin (UTF-8, belirtilen şema).
3. `python main.py` ile çalıştırın.

## Özellikler
- **Modlar**: Kart Ezber (flashcards), Çoktan Seçmeli (EN→TR, ters mod opsiyonel), Yaz-Boz (yazma pratiği, toleranslı eşleştirme), Hız Turu (zamanlı quiz).
- **Öğrenme**: SRS-lite ile tekrar planlama, günlük hedef (varsayılan 20).
- **Arayüz**: Sol menü (modlar), sağ panel (istatistikler, rozetler), koyu/açık tema, zoom, klavye kısayolları.
- **Veri**: Gömülü 20 kelime ile başlar; CSV içe aktarımı destekler.
- **İlerleme**: `storage/progress.json` otomatik kaydetme, dışa aktarma.
- **Testler**: `python -m unittest discover tests` ile çalıştırın (opsiyonel, kodda unittest import mevcut).

## Şema (words_2000.csv)
```
word,lemma,pos,definition,en_example,tr_translation,tr_example,frequency_rank
```
Örnek satırlar data/words_2000.csv'de mevcut.

## Hızlı Başlangıç
1. Uygulamayı çalıştırın: `python main.py`.
2. İlk açılışta gömülü kelimelerle oynayın (örn. "Kart Ezber" seçin).
3. Kelime gösterilir > Space ile çevir > B/N ile işaretle > Enter ile sonraki.
4. File > CSV İçe Aktar ile tam listeyi yükleyin.
5. Ayarlar'dan hedefi/temayı ayarlayın.
6. İstatistikleri sağ panelde izleyin; rozetler kazanın (örn. 100 kelime).

## Geliştirme Notları
- Kod PEP8 uyumlu, docstring'ler mevcut.
- Hatalar kullanıcı dostu mesajlarla yönetilir.
- İnternet gerektirmez; asenkron yükleme ile GUI donmaz.
- Ek: POS/frekans filtreleri (basit), ters mod, rozetler eklendi.

Sorunlar için: CSV şemasını kontrol edin veya progress.json'u silin (yeni profil).
```

#### Aşağıdaki gereksinimlerle Python dilinde, tek başına çalışabilen bir GUI kelime oyunu (İngilizce↔Türkçe) üret:  
####   
#### Teknoloji ve Yapı  
####   
#### Python 3.10+  
####   
#### GUI: Tkinter (harici bağımlılık yok). Modern görünüm için ttk kullan.  
####   
#### Dosya düzeni:  
####   
#### main.py (uygulama girişi)  
####   
#### data/words_2000.csv (kelime listesi)  
####   
#### assets/ (opsiyonel ikon/ses)  
####   
#### storage/progress.json (kullanıcı ilerlemesi)  
####   
#### Kod PEP8 uyumlu, iyi yorumlanmış ve fonksiyonlara ayrılmış olsun.  
####   
#### Veri (2000 en sık İngilizce kelime)  

I am creating a new standalone Python GUI application for an English-Turkish word game based on the provided requirements. The game allows users to practice translations in both directions (English to Turkish or Turkish to English) by displaying a random word in one language and prompting input in the other. It tracks progress by marking words as "known" after correct answers (3 consecutive correct translations in a session) and saves this to storage/progress.json. The UI uses Tkinter with ttk for a modern look, including a simple theme. Code is PEP8-compliant, modular with functions, and well-commented.

Key features:
- Loads words from data/words_2000.csv (English and Turkish columns).
- Randomly selects unknown words for practice.
- Modes: Toggle between English→Turkish and Turkish→English.
- Input validation, feedback via message boxes, score display.
- Progress persistence via JSON.
- No external dependencies beyond standard library.
- Sample CSV provided with 10 words (expand to 2000 common English words with translations for full use; sources like frequency lists and dictionaries can be used).

Directories like data/ and storage/ will be created if needed. Run with `python main.py`.

main.py
```
import csv
import json
import os
import random
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import ttk
from tkinter import messagebox


class WordGame(tk.Tk):
    """
    Main GUI application for English-Turkish word translation game.
    Uses Tkinter with ttk for modern styling.
    Tracks user progress in known words.
    """

    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()
        self.title("English-Turkish Word Game")
        self.geometry("500x400")
        self.resizable(False, False)

        # Style for modern look
        style = ttk.Style()
        style.theme_use("clam")  # Modern theme

        # Load data
        self.words = self._load_words()
        self.progress_file = "storage/progress.json"
        os.makedirs("storage", exist_ok=True)
        self.known_words = self._load_progress()
        self.current_word = None
        self.mode = "en_to_tr"  # Default: English to Turkish
        self.score = 0
        self.correct_streak = {}  # Track consecutive corrects per word

        # UI Setup
        self._setup_ui()

        # Initial word load
        self._load_new_word()

    def _load_words(self):
        """
        Load word list from CSV file.
        Returns list of dicts with 'en' and 'tr' keys.
        """
        words = []
        try:
            with open("data/words_2000.csv", "r", encoding="utf-8") as file:
                reader = csv.DictReader(file)
                for row in reader:
                    words.append({"en": row["english"].strip(), "tr": row["turkish"].strip()})
        except FileNotFoundError:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "data/words_2000.csv not found. Please add the file.")
            self.quit()
        return words

    def _load_progress(self):
        """
        Load known words from JSON progress file.
        Returns set of English words that are mastered.
        """
        if os.path.exists(self.progress_file):
            try:
                with open(self.progress_file, "r", encoding="utf-8") as file:
                    data = json.load(file)
                    return set(data)
            except (json.JSONDecodeError, KeyError):
                pass
        return set()

    def _save_progress(self):
        """
        Save known words to JSON progress file.
        """
        try:
            with open(self.progress_file, "w", encoding="utf-8") as file:
                json.dump(list(self.known_words), file, ensure_ascii=False, indent=4)
        except IOError:
            messagebox.showwarning("Warning", "Could not save progress.")

    def _setup_ui(self):
        """
        Set up the GUI elements using ttk for modern appearance.
        """
        # Main frame
        main_frame = ttk.Frame(self, padding="20")
        main_frame.grid(row=0, column=0, sticky=(tk.W, tk.E, tk.N, tk.S))

        # Title
        title_label = ttk.Label(main_frame, text="English ↔ Turkish Word Game", font=("Arial", 16, "bold"))
        title_label.grid(row=0, column=0, columnspan=2, pady=(0, 20))

        # Mode toggle
        self.mode_var = tk.StringVar(value="English to Turkish")
        mode_frame = ttk.Frame(main_frame)
        mode_frame.grid(row=1, column=0, columnspan=2, pady=(0, 10))
        ttk.Label(mode_frame, text="Mode:").grid(row=0, column=0, padx=(0, 5))
        mode_combo = ttk.Combobox(mode_frame, textvariable=self.mode_var, values=["English to Turkish", "Turkish to English"], state="readonly", width=20)
        mode_combo.grid(row=0, column=1)
        mode_combo.bind("<<ComboboxSelected>>", self._toggle_mode)

        # Current word display
        self.word_label = ttk.Label(main_frame, text="Word will appear here", font=("Arial", 14), foreground="blue")
        self.word_label.grid(row=2, column=0, columnspan=2, pady=(0, 10))

        # Instruction
        instr_label = ttk.Label(main_frame, text="Enter the translation:", font=("Arial", 10))
        instr_label.grid(row=3, column=0, columnspan=2, pady=(0, 5))

        # Input entry
        self.answer_entry = ttk.Entry(main_frame, font=("Arial", 12), width=30)
        self.answer_entry.grid(row=4, column=0, columnspan=2, pady=(0, 10))
        self.answer_entry.bind("<Return>", lambda event: self._check_answer())

        # Buttons frame
        button_frame = ttk.Frame(main_frame)
        button_frame.grid(row=5, column=0, columnspan=2, pady=(0, 20))

        self.check_button = ttk.Button(button_frame, text="Check Answer", command=self._check_answer)
        self.check_button.grid(row=0, column=0, padx=(0, 10))

        self.next_button = ttk.Button(button_frame, text="Next Word", command=self._load_new_word, state="disabled")
        self.next_button.grid(row=0, column=1)

        # Score and progress
        self.score_label = ttk.Label(main_frame, text="Score: 0 | Known Words: 0", font=("Arial", 10))
        self.score_label.grid(row=6, column=0, columnspan=2)

        # Quit button
        quit_button = ttk.Button(main_frame, text="Quit", command=self.quit)
        quit_button.grid(row=7, column=0, columnspan=2, pady=(20, 0))

    def _toggle_mode(self, event=None):
        """
        Toggle between translation modes.
        """
        if self.mode_var.get() == "English to Turkish":
            self.mode = "en_to_tr"
        else:
            self.mode = "tr_to_en"
        self._load_new_word()

    def _get_unknown_words(self):
        """
        Get list of words not yet known (for practice).
        """
        return [w for w in self.words if w["en"] not in self.known_words]

    def _load_new_word(self):
        """
        Load a random unknown word and display it.
        """
        unknown = self._get_unknown_words()
        if not unknown:
            messagebox.showinfo("Complete!", "You've mastered all words! Restarting progress.")
            self.known_words.clear()
            unknown = self.words

        self.current_word = random.choice(unknown)
        self.answer_entry.delete(0, tk.END)
        self.next_button.config(state="disabled")
        self.check_button.config(state="normal")

        if self.mode == "en_to_tr":
            display_text = self.current_word["en"]
            expected = self.current_word["tr"].lower()
        else:
            display_text = self.current_word["tr"]
            expected = self.current_word["en"].lower()

        self.word_label.config(text=display_text)
        self.correct_streak[self.current_word["en"]] = self.correct_streak.get(self.current_word["en"], 0)

        self._update_score_display()

    def _check_answer(self):
        """
        Check user's answer against expected translation.
        Provide feedback and update progress.
        """
        if not self.current_word:
            return

        user_answer = self.answer_entry.get().strip().lower()
        if self.mode == "en_to_tr":
            expected = self.current_word["tr"].lower()
            correct_feedback = f"Correct! Turkish: {self.current_word['tr']}"
        else:
            expected = self.current_word["en"].lower()
            correct_feedback = f"Correct! English: {self.current_word['en']}"

        if user_answer == expected:
            self.score += 1
            self.correct_streak[self.current_word["en"]] += 1
            if self.correct_streak[self.current_word["en"]] >= 3:
                self.known_words.add(self.current_word["en"])
                self._save_progress()
                messagebox.showinfo("Correct!", f"{correct_feedback}\nWord mastered!")
            else:
                messagebox.showinfo("Correct!", correct_feedback)
        else:
            self.correct_streak[self.current_word["en"]] = 0
            wrong_feedback = f"Wrong! The {self.mode.replace('_', ' ')} is: {expected.title()}"
            messagebox.showerror("Incorrect", wrong_feedback)
            self.score = max(0, self.score - 1)  # Penalty for wrong

        self.answer_entry.delete(0, tk.END)
        self.check_button.config(state="disabled")
        self.next_button.config(state="normal")
        self._update_score_display()

    def _update_score_display(self):
        """
        Update the score and known words display.
        """
        known_count = len(self.known_words)
        total_unknown = len(self._get_unknown_words())
        self.score_label.config(text=f"Score: {self.score} | Known: {known_count} | Remaining: {total_unknown}")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    app = WordGame()
    app.mainloop()
```

main.py
```
import csv
import json
import os
import random
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import ttk
from tkinter import messagebox


class WordGame(tk.Tk):
    """
    Main GUI application for English-Turkish word translation game.
    Uses Tkinter with ttk for modern styling.
    Passive review mode: displays word and pronunciation, reveals translation on button press.
    Tracks reviewed (known) words.
    """

    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()
        self.title("English-Turkish Word Game")
        self.geometry("500x450")
        self.resizable(False, False)

        # Style for modern look
        style = ttk.Style()
        style.theme_use("clam")  # Modern theme

        # Load data
        self.words = self._load_words()
        self.progress_file = "storage/progress.json"
        os.makedirs("storage", exist_ok=True)
        self.known_words = self._load_progress()
        self.current_word = None
        self.mode = "en_to_tr"  # Default: English to Turkish

        # UI Setup
        self._setup_ui()

        # Initial word load
        self._load_new_word()

    def _load_words(self):
        """
        Load word list from CSV file.
        Returns list of dicts with 'en', 'tr', 'en_pron', 'tr_pron' keys.
        """
        words = []
        try:
            with open("data/words_2000.csv", "r", encoding="utf-8") as file:
                reader = csv.DictReader(file)
                for row in reader:
                    words.append({
                        "en": row["english"].strip(),
                        "tr": row["turkish"].strip(),
                        "en_pron": row["english_pron"].strip(),
                        "tr_pron": row["turkish_pron"].strip()
                    })
        except FileNotFoundError:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "data/words_2000.csv not found. Please add the file.")
            self.quit()
        return words

    def _load_progress(self):
        """
        Load known words from JSON progress file.
        Returns set of English words that are reviewed/mastered.
        """
        if os.path.exists(self.progress_file):
            try:
                with open(self.progress_file, "r", encoding="utf-8") as file:
                    data = json.load(file)
                    return set(data)
            except (json.JSONDecodeError, KeyError):
                pass
        return set()

    def _save_progress(self):
        """
        Save known words to JSON progress file.
        """
        try:
            with open(self.progress_file, "w", encoding="utf-8") as file:
                json.dump(list(self.known_words), file, ensure_ascii=False, indent=4)
        except IOError:
            messagebox.showwarning("Warning", "Could not save progress.")

    def _setup_ui(self):
        """
        Set up the GUI elements using ttk for modern appearance.
        Passive review: no input, show source word/pron, reveal answer on button.
        """
        # Main frame
        main_frame = ttk.Frame(self, padding="20")
        main_frame.grid(row=0, column=0, sticky=(tk.W, tk.E, tk.N, tk.S))

        # Title
        title_label = ttk.Label(main_frame, text="English ↔ Turkish Word Review", font=("Arial", 16, "bold"))
        title_label.grid(row=0, column=0, columnspan=2, pady=(0, 20))

        # Mode toggle
        self.mode_var = tk.StringVar(value="English to Turkish")
        mode_frame = ttk.Frame(main_frame)
        mode_frame.grid(row=1, column=0, columnspan=2, pady=(0, 10))
        ttk.Label(mode_frame, text="Mode:").grid(row=0, column=0, padx=(0, 5))
        mode_combo = ttk.Combobox(mode_frame, textvariable=self.mode_var, values=["English to Turkish", "Turkish to English"], state="readonly", width=20)
        mode_combo.grid(row=0, column=1)
        mode_combo.bind("<<ComboboxSelected>>", self._toggle_mode)

        # Current word display
        self.word_label = ttk.Label(main_frame, text="Word will appear here", font=("Arial", 14), foreground="blue")
        self.word_label.grid(row=2, column=0, columnspan=2, pady=(0, 5))

        # Source pronunciation
        self.pron_label = ttk.Label(main_frame, text="", font=("Arial", 12, "italic"), foreground="green")
        self.pron_label.grid(row=3, column=0, columnspan=2, pady=(0, 10))

        # Answer section (initially hidden)
        answer_frame = ttk.Frame(main_frame)
        answer_frame.grid(row=4, column=0, columnspan=2, pady=(0, 10))
        self.answer_label = ttk.Label(answer_frame, text="", font=("Arial", 14), foreground="red")
        self.answer_label.grid(row=0, column=0, columnspan=2)
        self.answer_pron_label = ttk.Label(answer_frame, text="", font=("Arial", 12, "italic"), foreground="green")
        self.answer_pron_label.grid(row=1, column=0, columnspan=2, pady=(0, 5))

        # Buttons frame
        button_frame = ttk.Frame(main_frame)
        button_frame.grid(row=5, column=0, columnspan=2, pady=(0, 20))

        self.show_answer_button = ttk.Button(button_frame, text="Show Answer", command=self._show_answer)
        self.show_answer_button.grid(row=0, column=0, padx=(0, 10))

        self.next_button = ttk.Button(button_frame, text="Next Word", command=self._load_new_word, state="disabled")
        self.next_button.grid(row=0, column=1)

        # Progress display
        self.progress_label = ttk.Label(main_frame, text="Known Words: 0 | Remaining: 0", font=("Arial", 10))
        self.progress_label.grid(row=6, column=0, columnspan=2)

        # Quit button
        quit_button = ttk.Button(main_frame, text="Quit", command=self.quit)
        quit_button.grid(row=7, column=0, columnspan=2, pady=(20, 0))

        # Initially hide answer
        self._hide_answer()

    def _toggle_mode(self, event=None):
        """
        Toggle between translation modes.
        """
        if self.mode_var.get() == "English to Turkish":
            self.mode = "en_to_tr"
        else:
            self.mode = "tr_to_en"
        self._load_new_word()

    def _get_unknown_words(self):
        """
        Get list of words not yet known (for review).
        """
        return [w for w in self.words if w["en"] not in self.known_words]

    def _load_new_word(self):
        """
        Load a random unknown word and display source word/pron.
        Mark previous word as known if applicable.
        """
        if self.current_word and self.current_word["en"] not in self.known_words:
            self.known_words.add(self.current_word["en"])
            self._save_progress()

        unknown = self._get_unknown_words()
        if not unknown:
            messagebox.showinfo("Complete!", "You've reviewed all words! Restarting progress.")
            self.known_words.clear()
            self._save_progress()
            unknown = self.words

        self.current_word = random.choice(unknown)
        self._hide_answer()
        self.next_button.config(state="disabled")
        self.show_answer_button.config(state="normal")

        if self.mode == "en_to_tr":
            display_text = self.current_word["en"]
            display_pron = self.current_word["en_pron"]
            answer_text = self.current_word["tr"]
            answer_pron = self.current_word["tr_pron"]
        else:
            display_text = self.current_word["tr"]
            display_pron = self.current_word["tr_pron"]
            answer_text = self.current_word["en"]
            answer_pron = self.current_word["en_pron"]

        self.word_label.config(text=display_text)
        self.pron_label.config(text=f"Pronunciation: {display_pron}")
        self.answer_label.config(text=answer_text)
        self.answer_pron_label.config(text=f"Pronunciation: {answer_pron}")

        self._update_progress_display()

    def _show_answer(self):
        """
        Reveal the translation and its pronunciation.
        """
        self.answer_label.grid(row=0, column=0, columnspan=2)
        self.answer_pron_label.grid(row=1, column=0, columnspan=2, pady=(0, 5))
        self.show_answer_button.config(state="disabled")
        self.next_button.config(state="normal")

    def _hide_answer(self):
        """
        Hide the answer labels.
        """
        self.answer_label.grid_remove()
        self.answer_pron_label.grid_remove()
        self.show_answer_button.config(state="normal")

    def _update_progress_display(self):
        """
        Update the known words and remaining display.
        """
        known_count = len(self.known_words)
        total_unknown = len(self._get_unknown_words())
        self.progress_label.config(text=f"Known: {known_count} | Remaining: {total_unknown}")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    app = WordGame()
    app.mainloop()
```

```
import csv
import json
import os
import random
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import ttk
from tkinter import messagebox


class WordGame(tk.Tk):
    """
    Main GUI application for English-Turkish word translation game.
    Uses Tkinter with ttk for modern styling.
    Passive review mode: displays word and pronunciation (English only), reveals translation on button press.
    Tracks reviewed (known) words.
    """

    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()
        self.title("English-Turkish Word Game")
        self.geometry("500x450")
        self.resizable(False, False)

        # Style for modern look
        style = ttk.Style()
        style.theme_use("clam")  # Modern theme

        # Load data
        self.words = self._load_words()
        self.progress_file = "storage/progress.json"
        os.makedirs("storage", exist_ok=True)
        self.known_words = self._load_progress()
        self.current_word = None
        self.mode = "en_to_tr"  # Default: English to Turkish

        # UI Setup
        self._setup_ui()

        # Initial word load
        self._load_new_word()

    def _load_words(self):
        """
        Load word list from CSV file.
        Returns list of dicts with 'en', 'tr', 'en_pron' keys.
        """
        words = []
        try:
            with open("data/words_2000.csv", "r", encoding="utf-8") as file:
                reader = csv.DictReader(file)
                for row in reader:
                    words.append({
                        "en": row["english"].strip(),
                        "tr": row["turkish"].strip(),
                        "en_pron": row["english_pron"].strip()
                    })
        except FileNotFoundError:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "data/words_2000.csv not found. Please add the file.")
            self.quit()
        return words

    def _load_progress(self):
        """
        Load known words from JSON progress file.
        Returns set of English words that are reviewed/mastered.
        """
        if os.path.exists(self.progress_file):
            try:
                with open(self.progress_file, "r", encoding="utf-8") as file:
                    data = json.load(file)
                    return set(data)
            except (json.JSONDecodeError, KeyError):
                pass
        return set()

    def _save_progress(self):
        """
        Save known words to JSON progress file.
        """
        try:
            with open(self.progress_file, "w", encoding="utf-8") as file:
                json.dump(list(self.known_words), file, ensure_ascii=False, indent=4)
        except IOError:
            messagebox.showwarning("Warning", "Could not save progress.")

    def _setup_ui(self):
        """
        Set up the GUI elements using ttk for modern appearance.
        Passive review: no input, show source word/pron (English only), reveal answer on button.
        """
        # Main frame
        main_frame = ttk.Frame(self, padding="20")
        main_frame.grid(row=0, column=0, sticky=(tk.W, tk.E, tk.N, tk.S))

        # Title
        title_label = ttk.Label(main_frame, text="English ↔ Turkish Word Review", font=("Arial", 16, "bold"))
        title_label.grid(row=0, column=0, columnspan=2, pady=(0, 20))

        # Mode toggle
        self.mode_var = tk.StringVar(value="English to Turkish")
        mode_frame = ttk.Frame(main_frame)
        mode_frame.grid(row=1, column=0, columnspan=2, pady=(0, 10))
        ttk.Label(mode_frame, text="Mode:").grid(row=0, column=0, padx=(0, 5))
        mode_combo = ttk.Combobox(mode_frame, textvariable=self.mode_var, values=["English to Turkish", "Turkish to English"], state="readonly", width=20)
        mode_combo.grid(row=0, column=1)
        mode_combo.bind("<<ComboboxSelected>>", self._toggle_mode)

        # Current word display
        self.word_label = ttk.Label(main_frame, text="Word will appear here", font=("Arial", 14), foreground="blue")
        self.word_label.grid(row=2, column=0, columnspan=2, pady=(0, 5))

        # Source pronunciation (English only)
        self.pron_label = ttk.Label(main_frame, text="", font=("Arial", 12, "italic"), foreground="green")
        self.pron_label.grid(row=3, column=0, columnspan=2, pady=(0, 10))

        # Answer section (initially hidden)
        answer_frame = ttk.Frame(main_frame)
        answer_frame.grid(row=4, column=0, columnspan=2, pady=(0, 10))
        self.answer_label = ttk.Label(answer_frame, text="", font=("Arial", 14), foreground="red")
        self.answer_label.grid(row=0, column=0, columnspan=2)
        self.answer_pron_label = ttk.Label(answer_frame, text="", font=("Arial", 12, "italic"), foreground="green")
        self.answer_pron_label.grid(row=1, column=0, columnspan=2, pady=(0, 5))

        # Buttons frame
        button_frame = ttk.Frame(main_frame)
        button_frame.grid(row=5, column=0, columnspan=2, pady=(0, 20))

        self.show_answer_button = ttk.Button(button_frame, text="Show Answer", command=self._show_answer)
        self.show_answer_button.grid(row=0, column=0, padx=(0, 10))

        self.next_button = ttk.Button(button_frame, text="Next Word", command=self._load_new_word, state="disabled")
        self.next_button.grid(row=0, column=1)

        # Progress display
        self.progress_label = ttk.Label(main_frame, text="Known Words: 0 | Remaining: 0", font=("Arial", 10))
        self.progress_label.grid(row=6, column=0, columnspan=2)

        # Quit button
        quit_button = ttk.Button(main_frame, text="Quit", command=self.quit)
        quit_button.grid(row=7, column=0, columnspan=2, pady=(20, 0))

        # Initially hide answer
        self._hide_answer()

    def _toggle_mode(self, event=None):
        """
        Toggle between translation modes.
        """
        if self.mode_var.get() == "English to Turkish":
            self.mode = "en_to_tr"
        else:
            self.mode = "tr_to_en"
        self._load_new_word()

    def _get_unknown_words(self):
        """
        Get list of words not yet known (for review).
        """
        return [w for w in self.words if w["en"] not in self.known_words]

    def _load_new_word(self):
        """
        Load a random unknown word and display source word/pron (English only).
        Mark previous word as known if applicable.
        """
        if self.current_word and self.current_word["en"] not in self.known_words:
            self.known_words.add(self.current_word["en"])
            self._save_progress()

        unknown = self._get_unknown_words()
        if not unknown:
            messagebox.showinfo("Complete!", "You've reviewed all words! Restarting progress.")
            self.known_words.clear()
            self._save_progress()
            unknown = self.words

        self.current_word = random.choice(unknown)
        self._hide_answer()
        self.next_button.config(state="disabled")
        self.show_answer_button.config(state="normal")

        display_pron_text = ""
        answer_pron_text = ""

        if self.mode == "en_to_tr":
            display_text = self.current_word["en"]
            display_pron_text = f"Pronunciation: {self.current_word['en_pron']}"
            answer_text = self.current_word["tr"]
            # No Turkish pron
        else:
            display_text = self.current_word["tr"]
            # No Turkish pron
            answer_text = self.current_word["en"]
            answer_pron_text = f"Pronunciation: {self.current_word['en_pron']}"

        self.word_label.config(text=display_text)
        self.pron_label.config(text=display_pron_text)
        self.answer_label.config(text=answer_text)
        self.answer_pron_label.config(text=answer_pron_text)

        self._update_progress_display()

    def _show_answer(self):
        """
        Reveal the translation and its pronunciation (English only if applicable).
        """
        self.answer_label.grid(row=0, column=0, columnspan=2)
        if self.answer_pron_label.cget("text"):  # Only show if there's English pron
            self.answer_pron_label.grid(row=1, column=0, columnspan=2, pady=(0, 5))
        self.show_answer_button.config(state="disabled")
        self.next_button.config(state="normal")

    def _hide_answer(self):
        """
        Hide the answer labels.
        """
        self.answer_label.grid_remove()
        self.answer_pron_label.grid_remove()
        self.show_answer_button.config(state="normal")

    def _update_progress_display(self):
        """
        Update the known words and remaining display.
        """
        known_count = len(self.known_words)
        total_unknown = len(self._get_unknown_words())
        self.progress_label.config(text=f"Known: {known_count} | Remaining: {total_unknown}")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    app = WordGame()
    app.mainloop()
```

main.py
```
import csv
import os
import random
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import ttk
from tkinter import messagebox


class WordGame(tk.Tk):
    """
    Main GUI application for English-Turkish word translation game.
    Uses Tkinter with ttk for modern styling.
    Passive review mode: displays word and pronunciation (English only), reveals translation on button press.
    Tracks reviewed (known) words via CSV 'learned' flag.
    Manual marking with "I Learned It" button.
    """

    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()
        self.title("English-Turkish Word Game")
        self.geometry("500x450")
        self.resizable(False, False)

        # Style for modern look
        style = ttk.Style()
        style.theme_use("clam")  # Modern theme

        # Load data
        self.words = self._load_words()
        self.current_word = None
        self.mode = "en_to_tr"  # Default: English to Turkish
        self.known_words = {w["en"] for w in self.words if w["learned"] == 1}

        # UI Setup
        self._setup_ui()

        # Initial word load
        self._load_new_word()

    def _load_words(self):
        """
        Load word list from CSV file.
        Returns list of dicts with 'en', 'tr', 'en_pron', 'learned' keys.
        """
        words = []
        try:
            with open("data/words_2000.csv", "r", encoding="utf-8") as file:
                reader = csv.DictReader(file)
                for row in reader:
                    words.append({
                        "en": row["english"].strip(),
                        "tr": row["turkish"].strip(),
                        "en_pron": row["english_pron"].strip(),
                        "learned": int(row["learned"].strip())
                    })
        except FileNotFoundError:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "data/words_2000.csv not found. Please add the file.")
            self.quit()
        return words

    def _save_words_to_csv(self):
        """
        Save words list back to CSV file with learned flags.
        """
        try:
            with open("data/words_2000.csv", "w", newline="", encoding="utf-8") as file:
                fieldnames = ["english", "turkish", "english_pron", "learned"]
                writer = csv.DictWriter(file, fieldnames=fieldnames)
                writer.writeheader()
                for w in self.words:
                    writer.writerow({
                        "english": w["en"],
                        "turkish": w["tr"],
                        "english_pron": w["en_pron"],
                        "learned": w["learned"]
                    })
        except IOError:
            messagebox.showwarning("Warning", "Could not save to CSV.")

    def _setup_ui(self):
        """
        Set up the GUI elements using ttk for modern appearance.
        Passive review: no input, show source word/pron (English only), reveal answer on button.
        Add "I Learned It" button for manual marking.
        """
        # Main frame
        main_frame = ttk.Frame(self, padding="20")
        main_frame.grid(row=0, column=0, sticky=(tk.W, tk.E, tk.N, tk.S))

        # Title
        title_label = ttk.Label(main_frame, text="English ↔ Turkish Word Review", font=("Arial", 16, "bold"))
        title_label.grid(row=0, column=0, columnspan=3, pady=(0, 20))

        # Mode toggle
        self.mode_var = tk.StringVar(value="English to Turkish")
        mode_frame = ttk.Frame(main_frame)
        mode_frame.grid(row=1, column=0, columnspan=3, pady=(0, 10))
        ttk.Label(mode_frame, text="Mode:").grid(row=0, column=0, padx=(0, 5))
        mode_combo = ttk.Combobox(mode_frame, textvariable=self.mode_var, values=["English to Turkish", "Turkish to English"], state="readonly", width=20)
        mode_combo.grid(row=0, column=1)
        mode_combo.bind("<<ComboboxSelected>>", self._toggle_mode)

        # Current word display
        self.word_label = ttk.Label(main_frame, text="Word will appear here", font=("Arial", 14), foreground="blue")
        self.word_label.grid(row=2, column=0, columnspan=3, pady=(0, 5))

        # Source pronunciation (English only)
        self.pron_label = ttk.Label(main_frame, text="", font=("Arial", 12, "italic"), foreground="green")
        self.pron_label.grid(row=3, column=0, columnspan=3, pady=(0, 10))

        # Answer section (initially hidden)
        answer_frame = ttk.Frame(main_frame)
        answer_frame.grid(row=4, column=0, columnspan=3, pady=(0, 10))
        self.answer_label = ttk.Label(answer_frame, text="", font=("Arial", 14), foreground="red")
        self.answer_label.grid(row=0, column=0, columnspan=3)
        self.answer_pron_label = ttk.Label(answer_frame, text="", font=("Arial", 12, "italic"), foreground="green")
        self.answer_pron_label.grid(row=1, column=0, columnspan=3, pady=(0, 5))

        # Buttons frame
        button_frame = ttk.Frame(main_frame)
        button_frame.grid(row=5, column=0, columnspan=3, pady=(0, 20))

        self.show_answer_button = ttk.Button(button_frame, text="Show Answer", command=self._show_answer)
        self.show_answer_button.grid(row=0, column=0, padx=(0, 5))

        self.learned_button = ttk.Button(button_frame, text="I Learned It", command=self._mark_learned_and_next, state="disabled")
        self.learned_button.grid(row=0, column=1, padx=(0, 5))

        self.next_button = ttk.Button(button_frame, text="Next Word", command=self._load_new_word, state="disabled")
        self.next_button.grid(row=0, column=2)

        # Progress display
        self.progress_label = ttk.Label(main_frame, text="Known Words: 0 | Remaining: 0", font=("Arial", 10))
        self.progress_label.grid(row=6, column=0, columnspan=3)

        # Quit button
        quit_button = ttk.Button(main_frame, text="Quit", command=self.quit)
        quit_button.grid(row=7, column=0, columnspan=3, pady=(20, 0))

        # Initially hide answer
        self._hide_answer()

    def _toggle_mode(self, event=None):
        """
        Toggle between translation modes.
        """
        if self.mode_var.get() == "English to Turkish":
            self.mode = "en_to_tr"
        else:
            self.mode = "tr_to_en"
        self._load_new_word()

    def _get_unknown_words(self):
        """
        Get list of words not yet learned (learned == 0) for review.
        """
        return [w for w in self.words if w["learned"] == 0]

    def _load_new_word(self):
        """
        Load a random unknown word and display source word/pron (English only).
        No auto-marking; manual via button.
        """
        unknown = self._get_unknown_words()
        if not unknown:
            messagebox.showinfo("Complete!", "You've reviewed all words! Restarting progress.")
            for w in self.words:
                w["learned"] = 0
            self.known_words.clear()
            self._save_words_to_csv()
            unknown = self.words

        self.current_word = random.choice(unknown)
        self._hide_answer()
        self.next_button.config(state="disabled")
        self.learned_button.config(state="disabled")
        self.show_answer_button.config(state="normal")

        display_pron_text = ""
        answer_pron_text = ""

        if self.mode == "en_to_tr":
            display_text = self.current_word["en"]
            display_pron_text = f"Pronunciation: {self.current_word['en_pron']}"
            answer_text = self.current_word["tr"]
            # No Turkish pron
        else:
            display_text = self.current_word["tr"]
            # No Turkish pron
            answer_text = self.current_word["en"]
            answer_pron_text = f"Pronunciation: {self.current_word['en_pron']}"

        self.word_label.config(text=display_text)
        self.pron_label.config(text=display_pron_text)
        self.answer_label.config(text=answer_text)
        self.answer_pron_label.config(text=answer_pron_text)

        self._update_progress_display()

    def _mark_learned_and_next(self):
        """
        Mark current word as learned (set flag=1 in CSV), update known_words, save, then load next.
        """
        if not self.current_word:
            return
        en_word = self.current_word["en"]
        for w in self.words:
            if w["en"] == en_word:
                w["learned"] = 1
                break
        self.known_words.add(en_word)
        self._save_words_to_csv()
        self._load_new_word()

    def _show_answer(self):
        """
        Reveal the translation and its pronunciation (English only if applicable).
        Enable learned and next buttons.
        """
        self.answer_label.grid(row=0, column=0, columnspan=3)
        if self.answer_pron_label.cget("text"):  # Only show if there's English pron
            self.answer_pron_label.grid(row=1, column=0, columnspan=3, pady=(0, 5))
        self.show_answer_button.config(state="disabled")
        self.next_button.config(state="normal")
        self.learned_button.config(state="normal")

    def _hide_answer(self):
        """
        Hide the answer labels.
        """
        self.answer_label.grid_remove()
        self.answer_pron_label.grid_remove()
        self.show_answer_button.config(state="normal")

    def _update_progress_display(self):
        """
        Update the known words and remaining display.
        """
        known_count = len(self.known_words)
        remaining_count = len(self._get_unknown_words())
        self.progress_label.config(text=f"Known: {known_count} | Remaining: {remaining_count}")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    app = WordGame()
    app.mainloop()
```

main.py
```
import csv
import os
import random
import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import ttk
from tkinter import messagebox
from googletrans import Translator, LANGUAGES


class WordGame(tk.Tk):
    """
    Main GUI application for English-Turkish word translation game.
    Uses Tkinter with ttk for modern styling.
    Passive review mode: displays word and pronunciation (English only), reveals translation on button press.
    Tracks reviewed (known) words via CSV 'learned' flag.
    Manual marking with "I Learned It" button.
    Imports new words from mylist.txt with auto-translation on startup if file exists.
    """

    def __init__(self):
        super().__init__()
        self.title("English-Turkish Word Game")
        self.geometry("500x450")
        self.resizable(False, False)

        # Style for modern look
        style = ttk.Style()
        style.theme_use("clam")  # Modern theme

        # Load data
        self.words = self._load_words()
        self._import_from_mylist()  # Import new words if mylist.txt exists
        self.current_word = None
        self.mode = "en_to_tr"  # Default: English to Turkish
        self.known_words = {w["en"] for w in self.words if w["learned"] == 1}

        # UI Setup
        self._setup_ui()

        # Initial word load
        self._load_new_word()

    def _load_words(self):
        """
        Load word list from CSV file.
        Returns list of dicts with 'en', 'tr', 'en_pron', 'learned' keys.
        """
        words = []
        try:
            with open("data/words_2000.csv", "r", encoding="utf-8") as file:
                reader = csv.DictReader(file)
                for row in reader:
                    words.append({
                        "en": row["english"].strip(),
                        "tr": row["turkish"].strip(),
                        "en_pron": row["english_pron"].strip(),
                        "learned": int(row["learned"].strip())
                    })
        except FileNotFoundError:
            messagebox.showerror("Error", "data/words_2000.csv not found. Please add the file.")
            self.quit()
        return words

    def _import_from_mylist(self):
        """
        Read English words from mylist.txt (one per line), translate to Turkish using googletrans,
        check for duplicates, and append new entries to self.words and CSV with learned=0, en_pron=''.
        Runs only if mylist.txt exists.
        """
        mylist_path = "mylist.txt"
        if not os.path.exists(mylist_path):
            return

        translator = Translator()
        existing_ens = {w["en"].lower() for w in self.words}

        try:
            with open(mylist_path, "r", encoding="utf-8") as file:
                new_words = []
                for line in file:
                    en_word = line.strip()
                    if not en_word or en_word.lower() in existing_ens:
                        continue  # Skip empty or duplicates
                    try:
                        translation = translator.translate(en_word, src='en', dest='tr')
                        tr_word = translation.text.strip()
                        new_entry = {
                            "en": en_word,
                            "tr": tr_word,
                            "en_pron": "",
                            "learned": 0
                        }
                        new_words.append(new_entry)
                        existing_ens.add(en_word.lower())
                    except Exception as e:
                        messagebox.showwarning("Translation Error", f"Could not translate '{en_word}': {e}")
                        continue

            if new_words:
                self.words.extend(new_words)
                self._save_words_to_csv()
                messagebox.showinfo("Import Complete", f"Added {len(new_words)} new words from mylist.txt.")
        except IOError as e:
            messagebox.showerror("File Error", f"Could not read mylist.txt: {e}")

    def _save_words_to_csv(self):
        """
        Save words list back to CSV file with learned flags.
        """
        try:
            with open("data/words_2000.csv", "w", newline="", encoding="utf-8") as file:
                fieldnames = ["english", "turkish", "english_pron", "learned"]
                writer = csv.DictWriter(file, fieldnames=fieldnames)
                writer.writeheader()
                for w in self.words:
                    writer.writerow({
                        "english": w["en"],
                        "turkish": w["tr"],
                        "english_pron": w["en_pron"],
                        "learned": w["learned"]
                    })
        except IOError:
            messagebox.showwarning("Warning", "Could not save to CSV.")

    def _setup_ui(self):
        """
        Set up the GUI elements using ttk for modern appearance.
        Passive review: no input, show source word/pron (English only), reveal answer on button.
        Add "I Learned It" button for manual marking.
        """
        # Main frame
        main_frame = ttk.Frame(self, padding="20")
        main_frame.grid(row=0, column=0, sticky=(tk.W, tk.E, tk.N, tk.S))

        # Title
        title_label = ttk.Label(main_frame, text="English ↔ Turkish Word Review", font=("Arial", 16, "bold"))
        title_label.grid(row=0, column=0, columnspan=3, pady=(0, 20))

        # Mode toggle
        self.mode_var = tk.StringVar(value="English to Turkish")
        mode_frame = ttk.Frame(main_frame)
        mode_frame.grid(row=1, column=0, columnspan=3, pady=(0, 10))
        ttk.Label(mode_frame, text="Mode:").grid(row=0, column=0, padx=(0, 5))
        mode_combo = ttk.Combobox(mode_frame, textvariable=self.mode_var, values=["English to Turkish", "Turkish to English"], state="readonly", width=20)
        mode_combo.grid(row=0, column=1)
        mode_combo.bind("<<ComboboxSelected>>", self._toggle_mode)

        # Current word display
        self.word_label = ttk.Label(main_frame, text="Word will appear here", font=("Arial", 14), foreground="blue")
        self.word_label.grid(row=2, column=0, columnspan=3, pady=(0, 5))

        # Source pronunciation (English only)
        self.pron_label = ttk.Label(main_frame, text="", font=("Arial", 12, "italic"), foreground="green")
        self.pron_label.grid(row=3, column=0, columnspan=3, pady=(0, 10))

        # Answer section (initially hidden)
        answer_frame = ttk.Frame(main_frame)
        answer_frame.grid(row=4, column=0, columnspan=3, pady=(0, 10))
        self.answer_label = ttk.Label(answer_frame, text="", font=("Arial", 14), foreground="red")
        self.answer_label.grid(row=0, column=0, columnspan=3)
        self.answer_pron_label = ttk.Label(answer_frame, text="", font=("Arial", 12, "italic"), foreground="green")
        self.answer_pron_label.grid(row=1, column=0, columnspan=3, pady=(0, 5))

        # Buttons frame
        button_frame = ttk.Frame(main_frame)
        button_frame.grid(row=5, column=0, columnspan=3, pady=(0, 20))

        self.show_answer_button = ttk.Button(button_frame, text="Show Answer", command=self._show_answer)
        self.show_answer_button.grid(row=0, column=0, padx=(0, 5))

        self.learned_button = ttk.Button(button_frame, text="I Learned It", command=self._mark_learned_and_next, state="disabled")
        self.learned_button.grid(row=0, column=1, padx=(0, 5))

        self.next_button = ttk.Button(button_frame, text="Next Word", command=self._load_new_word, state="disabled")
        self.next_button.grid(row=0, column=2)

        # Progress display
        self.progress_label = ttk.Label(main_frame, text="Known Words: 0 | Remaining: 0", font=("Arial", 10))
        self.progress_label.grid(row=6, column=0, columnspan=3)

        # Quit button
        quit_button = ttk.Button(main_frame, text="Quit", command=self.quit)
        quit_button.grid(row=7, column=0, columnspan=3, pady=(20, 0))

        # Initially hide answer
        self._hide_answer()

    def _toggle_mode(self, event=None):
        """
        Toggle between translation modes.
        """
        if self.mode_var.get() == "English to Turkish":
            self.mode = "en_to_tr"
        else:
            self.mode = "tr_to_en"
        self._load_new_word()

    def _get_unknown_words(self):
        """
        Get list of words not yet learned (learned == 0) for review.
        """
        return [w for w in self.words if w["learned"] == 0]

    def _load_new_word(self):
        """
        Load a random unknown word and display source word/pron (English only).
        No auto-marking; manual via button.
        """
        unknown = self._get_unknown_words()
        if not unknown:
            messagebox.showinfo("Complete!", "You've reviewed all words! Restarting progress.")
            for w in self.words:
                w["learned"] = 0
            self.known_words.clear()
            self._save_words_to_csv()
            unknown = self.words

        self.current_word = random.choice(unknown)
        self._hide_answer()
        self.next_button.config(state="disabled")
        self.learned_button.config(state="disabled")
        self.show_answer_button.config(state="normal")

        display_pron_text = ""
        answer_pron_text = ""

        if self.mode == "en_to_tr":
            display_text = self.current_word["en"]
            display_pron_text = f"Pronunciation: {self.current_word['en_pron']}"
            answer_text = self.current_word["tr"]
            # No Turkish pron
        else:
            display_text = self.current_word["tr"]
            # No Turkish pron
            answer_text = self.current_word["en"]
            answer_pron_text = f"Pronunciation: {self.current_word['en_pron']}"

        self.word_label.config(text=display_text)
        self.pron_label.config(text=display_pron_text)
        self.answer_label.config(text=answer_text)
        self.answer_pron_label.config(text=answer_pron_text)

        self._update_progress_display()

    def _mark_learned_and_next(self):
        """
        Mark current word as learned (set flag=1 in CSV), update known_words, save, then load next.
        """
        if not self.current_word:
            return
        en_word = self.current_word["en"]
        for w in self.words:
            if w["en"] == en_word:
                w["learned"] = 1
                break
        self.known_words.add(en_word)
        self._save_words_to_csv()
        self._load_new_word()

    def _show_answer(self):
        """
        Reveal the translation and its pronunciation (English only if applicable).
        Enable learned and next buttons.
        """
        self.answer_label.grid(row=0, column=0, columnspan=3)
        if self.answer_pron_label.cget("text"):  # Only show if there's English pron
            self.answer_pron_label.grid(row=1, column=0, columnspan=3, pady=(0, 5))
        self.show_answer_button.config(state="disabled")
        self.next_button.config(state="normal")
        self.learned_button.config(state="normal")

    def _hide_answer(self):
        """
        Hide the answer labels.
        """
        self.answer_label.grid_remove()
        self.answer_pron_label.grid_remove()
        self.show_answer_button.config(state="normal")

    def _update_progress_display(self):
        """
        Update the known words and remaining display.
        """
        known_count = len(self.known_words)
        remaining_count = len(self._get_unknown_words())
        self.progress_label.config(text=f"Known: {known_count} | Remaining: {remaining_count}")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    app = WordGame()
    app.mainloop()
```
